package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(12, 33));
            System.out.println(min(-20, 0));
            System.out.println(min(-10, -20));
    }
}
2.8.2
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }
}

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}
Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 2
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(convertEurToUsd(60, 1.16));
        System.out.println(convertEurToUsd(6, 1.16));
    }
    public static double convertEurToUsd(int eur, double exchangeRate) {

        double convertEurToUsd = eur * exchangeRate;
        return convertEurToUsd;
    }

}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0318;
import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String sAge = reader.readLine();
        int nAge = Integer.parseInt(sAge);
        String name = reader.readLine();
    System.out.println(name + " захватит мир через " + nAge + " лет. Му-ха-ха!");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String name = reader.readLine();
        String sAge1 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge1 = Integer.parseInt(sAge1);
        String sAge2 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge2 = Integer.parseInt(sAge2);
        System.out.println(name + "получает" + nAge1 + "через" + nAge2 + "лет.");
    }
}

3.11.3
package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
            public static void main(String[] args) {
            Person person = new Person();
            System.out.println("Age is: " + person.age);
            person.abjustAge(person.age);
            System.out.println("Adjust age is: " + person.age);
        }
        public static class Person {
            public int age = 20;

            public void abjustAge(int age) {
                this.age = age + 20;
                System.out.println("Age in adjustAge() is: " + age);

            }
        }
   }

public class Solution {
            public static void main(String[] args) {
            Apple apple = new Apple();
            apple.addlePrice(50);
            Apple apple2 = new Apple();
            apple2.addlePrice(100);
                System.out.println("Стоимость яблок " + Apple.applesPrice);
        }
        public static class Apple{
            public static int applesPrice = 0;

            public static void addlePrice(int applesPrice) {
                Apple.applesPrice = Apple.applesPrice + applesPrice;
            }
        }
   }

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

        System.out.println(convertCelsiusToFahrenheit(41));
    }

        double a;

        return a;

                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {

2.8.2
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }
}

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}
Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 2
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0318;
import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String sAge = reader.readLine();
        int nAge = Integer.parseInt(sAge);
        String name = reader.readLine();
    System.out.println(name + " захватит мир через " + nAge + " лет. Му-ха-ха!");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String name = reader.readLine();
        String sAge1 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge1 = Integer.parseInt(sAge1);
        String sAge2 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge2 = Integer.parseInt(sAge2);
        System.out.println(name + "получает" + nAge1 + "через" + nAge2 + "лет.");
    }
}

3.11.3
package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
            public static void main(String[] args) {
            Person person = new Person();
            System.out.println("Age is: " + person.age);
            person.abjustAge(person.age);
            System.out.println("Adjust age is: " + person.age);
        }
        public static class Person {
            public int age = 20;

            public void abjustAge(int age) {
                this.age = age + 20;
                System.out.println("Age in adjustAge() is: " + age);

            }
        }
   }

            Apple apple2 = new Apple();
            apple2.addlePrice(100);
                System.out.println("Стоимость яблок " + Apple.applesPrice);
        }
        public static class Apple{
            public static int applesPrice = 0;

            public static void addlePrice(int applesPrice) {
                Apple.applesPrice = Apple.applesPrice + applesPrice;
            }
        }

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(12, 33));
            System.out.println(min(-20, 0));
            System.out.println(min(-10, -20));
    }
}
2.8.2
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }
}

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}
Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 2
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(convertEurToUsd(60, 1.16));
        System.out.println(convertEurToUsd(6, 1.16));
    }
    public static double convertEurToUsd(int eur, double exchangeRate) {

        double convertEurToUsd = eur * exchangeRate;
        return convertEurToUsd;
    }

}

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(addTenPercent(9));
    }
    public static double addTenPercent(int i) {

        double addTenPercent = i + i * 0.1;
        return addTenPercent;
    }

}

import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String sAge = reader.readLine();
        int nAge = Integer.parseInt(sAge);
        String name = reader.readLine();
    System.out.println(name + " захватит мир через " + nAge + " лет. Му-ха-ха!");
    }
}

import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String name = reader.readLine();
        String sAge1 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge1 = Integer.parseInt(sAge1);
        String sAge2 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge2 = Integer.parseInt(sAge2);
        System.out.println(name + "получает" + nAge1 + "через" + nAge2 + "лет.");
    }
}

3.11.3
package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
            public static void main(String[] args) {
            Person person = new Person();
            System.out.println("Age is: " + person.age);
            person.abjustAge(person.age);
            System.out.println("Adjust age is: " + person.age);
        }
        public static class Person {
            public int age = 20;

            public void abjustAge(int age) {
                this.age = age + 20;
                System.out.println("Age in adjustAge() is: " + age);

            }
        }
   }

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(12, 33));
            System.out.println(min(-20, 0));
            System.out.println(min(-10, -20));
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }
}

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}
Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 2
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(convertEurToUsd(60, 1.16));
        System.out.println(convertEurToUsd(6, 1.16));
    }
    public static double convertEurToUsd(int eur, double exchangeRate) {

        double convertEurToUsd = eur * exchangeRate;
        return convertEurToUsd;
    }

}

import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String sAge = reader.readLine();
        int nAge = Integer.parseInt(sAge);
        String name = reader.readLine();
    System.out.println(name + " захватит мир через " + nAge + " лет. Му-ха-ха!");
    }

import java.io.InputStreamReader;
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String name = reader.readLine();
        String sAge1 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge1 = Integer.parseInt(sAge1);
        String sAge2 = reader.readLine();
        int nAge2 = Integer.parseInt(sAge2);
        System.out.println(name + "получает" + nAge1 + "через" + nAge2 + "лет.");
    }
}

3.11.3
package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
            public static void main(String[] args) {
            Person person = new Person();
            System.out.println("Age is: " + person.age);
            person.abjustAge(person.age);
            System.out.println("Adjust age is: " + person.age);
        }
        public static class Person {
            public int age = 20;

            public void abjustAge(int age) {
                this.age = age + 20;
                System.out.println("Age in adjustAge() is: " + age);

            }
        }
   }

            Apple apple2 = new Apple();
            apple2.addlePrice(100);
                System.out.println("Стоимость яблок " + Apple.applesPrice);
        }
        public static class Apple{
            public static int applesPrice = 0;

            public static void addlePrice(int applesPrice) {
                Apple.applesPrice = Apple.applesPrice + applesPrice;
            }
        }

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(convertCelsiusToFahrenheit(41));
    }
    public static double convertCelsiusToFahrenheit(int celsius) {
        double a;
        a = ( 9.0 / 5.0 ) * celsius + 32.0;
        return a;
    }

                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(12, 33));
            System.out.println(min(-20, 0));
            System.out.println(min(-10, -20));

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

/*
 */
public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }
}

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

3.11.3
package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

            person.abjustAge(person.age);
            System.out.println("Adjust age is: " + person.age);
        }
        public static class Person {
            public int age = 20;

            public void abjustAge(int age) {
                this.age = age + 20;
                System.out.println("Age in adjustAge() is: " + age);

            }
        }
   }

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(12, 33));
            System.out.println(min(-20, 0));
            System.out.println(min(-10, -20));

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

/*
 */
public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }
}

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}

4.7.3
public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception{
        BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        String e = reader.readLine();
        int a = Integer.parseInt(e);
        int c = a / 2;
        double b = a / 2.0;
        int f = e.length();
        boolean s = (a >= 1 && a <= 999);
        if (s) {
            if (f == 1 && b == c)
                System.out.println("четное однозначное число");
            else {
                if (f == 1 && b != c)
                    System.out.println("нечетное однозначное число");
                else {
                    if (f == 2 && b == c)
                        System.out.println("четное двузначное число");
                    else {
                        if (f == 2 && b != c)
                            System.out.println("нечетное двузначное число");
                        else {
                            if (f == 3 && b == c)
                                System.out.println("четное трехзначное число");
                            else
                                System.out.println("нечетное трехзначное число");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task04.task0417;
import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.InputStreamReader;
import java.io.Reader;

public class Solution {

            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(12, 33));
            System.out.println(min(-20, 0));
            System.out.println(min(-10, -20));

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Solution {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
            int m2;
            if(a < c)
                m2 = a;
            else
                m2 = c;
            int m3;
            if(m < m2)
                m3 = m;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println(min(1, 2, 3));
            System.out.println(min(-1, -2, -3));
            System.out.println(min(5, 5, 10));
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
        public static int min(int a, int b, int c, int d) {
            int m2;
            if(c < d)
                m2 = c;
            else
                m2 = d;
            int m3;
            int r = min(a, b);
            if(r < m2)
                m3 = r;
            else
                m3 = m2;
            return m3;
        }
        public static int min(int a, int b) {
            int m;
            if(a < b)
                m = a;
            else
                m = b;
        return m;
        }
        public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10));
            System.out.println(min(-40, -10, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -40, -30, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -40, 40));
            System.out.println(min(-20, -10, -30, -40));
    }
}

Лекция 2 СПЕЦИАЛЬНОЕ ЗАДАНИЕ 1
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class Artifact {
       int serialNumber;
       String culture;
       int centery;
       static int count = 212121;

       public Artifact() {
       this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture) {
           this.culture = culture;
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
       }
       public Artifact(String culture, int centery) {
           this.serialNumber = ++count;
           this.culture = culture;
           this.centery = centery;
       }
       public static void main(String[] args) {
           Artifact artifact1 = new Artifact();
           Artifact artifact2 = new Artifact("Ацтеков");
           Artifact artifact3 = new Artifact("Ацтеков", 12);
           System.out.println("Создан первый артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact1.serialNumber);
           System.out.println("Создан второй артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact2.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact2.culture);
           System.out.println("Создан третий артефакт, с серийным номером " + artifact3.serialNumber + ", принадлежащий к культуре " + artifact3.culture + ". Находка датируется " + artifact3.centery +" веком н.э.");
       }
}

package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;
/*
 */
public class User {
    String name;
    int age;
    double heigh;

    public User(String name, int age, double heigh) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(String name, double heigh, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(int age, String name, double heigh) {
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
        this.heigh = heigh;
    }
    public User(int age, double heigh, String name) {
        this.age = age;
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public User(double heigh, String name, int age) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }
    public User(double heigh, int age, String name) {
        this.heigh = heigh;
        this.age = age;
        this.name = name;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        User user1 = new User("Вася", 180.2, 18);
        User user2 = new User(19, "Маша", 164.6);
        System.out.println(user2.name);
    }
}
Лекция про методы jarvis
package com.javarush.task.task01.task0114;

public class Jarvis {

    public void sayHi(String...names) {

        for (String name: names) {
            System.out.println("Добрый вечер, " + name + ", как ваши дела?");
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Jarvis jarvis = new Jarvis();
        jarvis.sayHi("Дима");
    }
}

package com.javarush.task.task03.task0324;

public class Solution {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println(sumDigitsInNumber(546));
    }
    public static int sumDigitsInNumber(int number) {
        int a = number / 100;
        int b = (number - a * 100) / 10;
        int c = number - a * 100 - b * 10;
        int sumDigitsInNumber = a + b + c;
        return sumDigitsInNumber;
    }
}
